<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жида́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-židátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to expect, to anticipate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидать.html>ожида́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстрый.html>бы́строй</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ды</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My ne <b>ožidáli</b> takój býstroj pobédy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We didn’t <b>expect</b> such a quick victory.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидающийся.html>ожида́ющийся</a> (7739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидающийся.html>ожида́ющийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ožidájuščijsja</span>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озабоченный.html>озабо́ченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozabóčennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озаботить.html>озабо́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ozabótitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озабоченный.html>озабо́ченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozabóčennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>preoccupied
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сексуальный.html>сексуа́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:озабоченный.html>озабо́ченный</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sɛksuálʹno <b>ozabóčennyj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">preoccupied with sex, hot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>anxious, worried</li></ol>

***озадачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:озадачивать.html>озада́чивать</a> (31393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озадачить.html>озада́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ozadáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озадачивать.html>озада́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozadáčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озадачить.html>озада́чить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to puzzle, to perplex
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:озадачивать.html>озада́чивать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ozadáčivatʹ</b> kovó-libo voprósom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to puzzle smb with a question</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give a task/job</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́ча</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadáča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give a task/job</li></ol>

***озарить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:озарить.html>озари́ть</a> (8637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>заря́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озарить.html>озари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озарять.html>озаря́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to light up; to illuminate</li>
<li>to brighten, to lighten</li>
<li><i>thought or idea</i> to strike, to dawn up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:озарить.html>озари́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>ozarílo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it dawned upon him</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***озарять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:озарять.html>озаря́ть</a> (15643)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озарить.html>озари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ozarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озарять.html>озаря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozarjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озарить.html>озари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to light up; to illuminate</li>
<li>to brighten, to lighten</li>
<li><i>thought or idea</i> to strike, to dawn up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:озарить.html>озари́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó ozarílo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it dawned upon him</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***озвереть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:озвереть.html>озвере́ть</a> (13860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звереть.html>звере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zverétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озвереть.html>озвере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozverétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звереть.html>звере́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fly into a rage</li>
<li>to become a beast, to become brutalized</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run wild, to run riot, to go crazy, to go nuts
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:озвереть.html>озвере́ли</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy što, <b>ozveréli</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Have you gone crazy?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***озвучить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:озвучить.html>озву́чить</a> (25448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>звук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvuk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озвучить.html>озву́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozvúčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">озву́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dub, to post-synch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:озвучить.html>озву́чить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:синхронно.html>синхро́нно</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ozvúčitʹ</b> sinxrónno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lip-synch; mouth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to voice, to give utterance <i>(to)</i>, to read</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>звук</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zvuk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">оздорови́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ozdorovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оздоровительный.html>оздорови́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozdorovítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>health-improving
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оздоровительный.html>оздорови́тельные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мероприятие.html>мероприя́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ozdorovítelʹnyje</b> meroprijátija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">health promotion program</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оздоровительный.html>оздорови́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лагерь.html>ла́герь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">détskij <b>ozdorovítelʹnyj</b> lágerʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">children's health camp</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оздоровительный.html>оздорови́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клуб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ozdorovítelʹnyj</b> klub</i> ― <span class="e-translation">health club</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оздоровление.html>оздоровле́ние</a> (26027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">оздорови́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ozdorovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***оземь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оземь.html>о́земь</a> (32107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ob zemь</i>, the latter part an alternative form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zemľa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth, land</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оземь.html>о́земь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ózemʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> against the ground
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1872</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a> (Leo Tolstoy),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:кавказский.html>Кавка́зский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пленник.html>пле́нник</a></cite>  | <cite>Prisoner of the Caucasus</cite> |  | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=-Sk1AQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA9amp;lpg=PA9amp;dq=%22%D0%BE%D0%B7%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%8C%22">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́рилась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шадь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оземь.html>о́земь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>ма́ху</a>,—навали́лась жи́лину <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Udárilasʹ lóšadʹ <b>ózemʹ</b> so vsevó máxu,—navalílasʹ Žílinu ná nogu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The horse hit <b>the ground</b> with all its weight, and fell on Zhilin's leg.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="поэтическое"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a>.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>Тут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́рился</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:оземь.html>о́земь</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затем.html>зате́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>помню</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мно́ю</a> дальше <a href = vnd.unilang:случиться.html>случи́лось</a>! </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***озираться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:озираться.html>озира́ться</a> (5437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озираться.html>озира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to look around (oneself)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">

***озлобить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:озлобить.html>озло́бить</a> (19097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlóba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or less likely from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зло́бить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlóbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озлобить.html>озло́бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ozlóbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озлобление.html>озлобле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ozloblénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озлобление.html>озлобле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озлобление.html>озлобле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озлобление.html>озлобле́ний</a></b>)
